Relationship Last 180 Day #

On-chain Communities Relationship Graph

Communities CSV

Legend: Dot represent regular accounts, square represent validator addresses. Triangles represent regular accounts hat have interacted with known public addresses.

Edge thickness indicates interaction volume, which combines amounts from all operations: transfer, reward, bond, withdraw.

A community represents a group of related addresses that interact with each other during a specific time period, but this does not necessarily mean they belong to the same person. The on-chain relationship graph has already excluded some known public addresses.

Community ID is computed and has no correlational relationship across different graph structures. It only serves to differentiate communities within the current graph.

Double-click a node to navigate to that address’s blockchain explorer.
